.         drop time

.         collapse (mean) p* sp* onsite_insp_hours hours dv* (firstnm) state sample_pp, by(mineid year)
.         rename year time
.         encode time, gen(time2)
.         drop time
.         rename time2 time
.         bys mineid: gen mine_time = _n
.         
.         pause "complete: year_avg collapse"
. }
